## <a name="windows-server-2012-extended-rights"></a><span data-ttu-id="e110c-2904">Derechos extendidos de Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e110c-2904">Windows Server 2012 Extended Rights</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e110c-2905">Esta clase contiene los siguientes derechos extendidos para Windows Server 2012:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e110c-2905">This class contains the following extended rights for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="e110c-2906">Nombre común</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e110c-2906">Common Name</span></span>                                                                    |
